plane-crazy 2021-10-01 17:14:29 A zip bomb, also known as a decompression bomb or zip of death is a malicious archive file designed to crash or render useless the program or system reading it. It is often employed to disable antivirus software, in order to create an opening for more traditional viruses.[1]

Rather than hijacking the normal operation of the program, a zip bomb allows the program to work as intended, but the archive is crafted so that unpacking it (e.g., by a virus scanner in order to scan for viruses) requires inordinate amounts of time, disk space and/or memory.
